# Prometheus Lua Obfuscator

**Based on [Prometheus](https://github.com/prometheus-lua/Prometheus) by Elias Oelschner.**

**Lua obfuscator:** feed it a Lua script and it runs it through a configurable pipeline, then outputs one obfuscated `.lua` file. No native deps—pure Lua, runs under **LuaJIT** or **Lua 5.1+**.

The pipeline turns your code into something much harder to read, debug, or dump:

- **Custom VM bytecode** — your logic is compiled into a small custom instruction set and executed by a tiny VM in the output; the original control flow and structure are no longer visible in the script.
- **Constant arrays** — literals (strings, numbers) are moved into packed arrays and accessed by index; constants are shuffled and decoded at runtime so static inspection doesn’t show the real values.
- **String encryption** — string literals are encrypted (e.g. octal/byte encoding) and decoded on the fly; env dumps and simple greps won’t reveal plaintext.
- **Anti-tamper** — integrity checks and structural tricks make patching or modifying the obfuscated script risky (e.g. break the script or trigger traps).
- **Watermark checks** — optional watermarking and runtime checks tie the code to a specific build or discourage stripping/copying.
- **Number obfuscation** — numeric constants are replaced with arithmetic expressions or table lookups so numbers aren’t sitting in the source in plain form.

You get a single, portable `.lua` file that behaves like the original but is far harder to reverse, log, or dump in a useful way.

**CHANGES FROM ORIGINAL UPSTREAM** — This fork is not the same as stock Prometheus. Tweaks and additions make the output much harder to:

- **Deobfuscate** — harder to reverse and reconstruct original source (VM, constant encoding, control flow).

- **Env log / dump** — mitigations so env dumps and runtime logging don’t expose the real logic or strings in a usable form.

- **Tamper with or analyze** — anti-tamper and watermark checks; output structure differs so tools tuned for stock Prometheus don’t apply as-is.

- **Infinite loop trap** — added to crash the dumper/env logger and to hinder automated analysis and stepping through the obfuscated code.

# OUTPUT EXAMPLE ( 2K LINES OF LUA CODE OBFUSCATED )

